Kanbans are moved across the board to the IN_PROGRES queue and worked on until the are completed and then moved to the final completed (\"DONE\") queue.\r\n\r\n\r\nBoards:\r\nA Kanban \"board\" literally can represent everything you want it to be: a simple shopping list, a work project, an event, you know... everything.\r\n\r\n\r\nTasks and their States:\r\nYou assign your Tasks to a Board.
